--- Example 3: Efficiency Comparison ---
Without Index (Linear Scan):
  - Must scan all 26651 records
  - Must access all 144 data blocks
  - Time complexity: O(n)
With B+ Tree Index:
  - Tree height: 2 levels
  - Index nodes accessed: ~2 nodes
  - Data blocks accessed: Only blocks containing matching records
  - Time complexity: O(log n)
